__bootstrap:
	NEW_SCOPE
	BEGIN_STRUCT dpu_set_t
	APPEND_INT 0 foo
	END_STRUCT
	NEW_GLOBAL_INT 0 NUM_DPUS
	GET_IDENTIFIER NUM_DPUS
	PUSH_INT 128
	ASSIGN
	NEW_GLOBAL_INT 0 NUM_TASKLETS
	GET_IDENTIFIER NUM_TASKLETS
	PUSH_INT 16
	ASSIGN
	NEW_GLOBAL_INT 0 DATA_PREP_PARAMS
	GET_IDENTIFIER DATA_PREP_PARAMS
	PUSH_INT 2097152
	ASSIGN
	BEGIN_STRUCT dpu_arguments_t
	APPEND_INT 0 size
	APPEND_INT 0 kernel
	APPEND_LONG 0 t_count
	END_STRUCT
	BEGIN_STRUCT dpu_results_t
	APPEND_LONG 0 cycles
	APPEND_LONG 0 t_count
	END_STRUCT
	CALL main
	DELETE_SCOPE
read_input:
	NEW_SCOPE
	NEW_SCOPE
	NEW_FAST_INT 0 i
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	PUSH_INT 0
	ASSIGN
	JUMP L0
L0:
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	GET_IDENTIFIER nr_elements
	LESS
	JUMP_IF_NONZERO L1
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	GET_IDENTIFIER nr_elements
	LESS
	JUMP_IF_ZERO L2
L1:
	NEW_SCOPE
	GET_IDENTIFIER A
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	GET_SUBSCRIPT
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	PUSH_INT 100
	MOD
	ASSIGN
	DELETE_SCOPE
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	ASSIGN_PLUS_PLUS
	JUMP L0
L2:
	DELETE_SCOPE
	DELETE_SCOPE
reduction_host:
	NEW_SCOPE
	NEW_FAST_LONG 0 count
	GET_IDENTIFIER count
	PUSH_INT 0
	ASSIGN
	NEW_SCOPE
	NEW_FAST_INT 0 i
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	PUSH_INT 0
	ASSIGN
	JUMP L3
L3:
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	GET_IDENTIFIER nr_elements
	LESS
	JUMP_IF_NONZERO L4
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	GET_IDENTIFIER nr_elements
	LESS
	JUMP_IF_ZERO L5
L4:
	NEW_SCOPE
	GET_IDENTIFIER count
	GET_IDENTIFIER A
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	GET_SUBSCRIPT
	ASSIGN_ADD
	DELETE_SCOPE
	GET_IDENTIFIER i
	ASSIGN_PLUS_PLUS
	JUMP L3
L5:
	DELETE_SCOPE
	NEW_RETURN_LONG 0
	GET_IDENTIFIER count
	ASSIGN_RETURN
	RETURN
	DELETE_SCOPE
roundup:
	NEW_SCOPE
	NEW_RETURN_INT 0
	GET_IDENTIFIER n
	GET_IDENTIFIER m
	DIV
	GET_IDENTIFIER m
	MUL
	GET_IDENTIFIER m
	ADD
	ASSIGN_RETURN
	RETURN
	DELETE_SCOPE
divceil:
	NEW_SCOPE
	NEW_RETURN_INT 0
	GET_IDENTIFIER n
	PUSH_INT 1
	SUB
	GET_IDENTIFIER m
	DIV
	PUSH_INT 1
	ADD
	ASSIGN_RETURN
	RETURN
	DELETE_SCOPE

	SIZEOF_LONG 0
